<div id="review_237314554" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/237314554" />
    <a title="Brett Talley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6030342-brett-talley"><img alt="Brett Talley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442598514p2/6030342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/237314554?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brett Talley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brett Talley" href="/user/show/6030342-brett-talley">Brett Talley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer237314554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14145380624682181868">As with most reviews, there be spoilers ahead. <br/><br/>Dean Koontz is probably one of the five most famous authors in America, and his legion of fans speaks to his ability to tap into some thread of humanity and for that, he should be praised. People who hate Dean Koontz like to act as though he can't string words together into a sentence, but you don't sell millions of books on hype and marketing alone. Whatever it is about Koontz that makes him successful, Phantoms is one of the books that launched hi</span>
  <span id="freeText14145380624682181868" style="display:none">As with most reviews, there be spoilers ahead. <br /><br />Dean Koontz is probably one of the five most famous authors in America, and his legion of fans speaks to his ability to tap into some thread of humanity and for that, he should be praised. People who hate Dean Koontz like to act as though he can't string words together into a sentence, but you don't sell millions of books on hype and marketing alone. Whatever it is about Koontz that makes him successful, Phantoms is one of the books that launched him into the stratosphere. But while Koontz has an undeniable appeal to some people, I am not really one of them. It doesn't help that I have heard him lament the success of Phantoms because it transformed him into a horror writer when he really wanted to work on thrillers and mysteries. I am sure the thousands of published authors who maintain a full time job just to eat feel his pain. <br /><br />I think the success of Phantoms can be traced to what is a truly brilliant premise. A woman picks up her sister at the airport. Upon returning to the small mountain town in which she lives, they find it eerily quiet and deserted. Every single person has vanished. We soon discover that an ancient entity, older than the dinosaurs, has come to this sleepy little hamlet to feast, as it does every few thousand years.<br /><br />Now that is a great premise. I would kill to have thought of it, and frankly, the premise is enough to get you through the entire book. But pretty much everything else fails. The plotting is erratic, the characters underdeveloped, the dialogue trite and unbelievable. I think my least favorite character is the leader of a biker gang—who also happens to be a Satanist—who makes the bikers in the original Dawn of the Dead look like reasonable and serious portrayals. <br /><br />For what it is, Phantoms serves its purpose. It's not like I didn't finish it. Just don't expect much more than a great premise, and you should be fine. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14145380624682181868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Mike (the Paladin)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2187043-mike-the-paladin"><img alt="Mike (the Paladin)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528431476p2/2187043.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780425101452" href="/book/show/904639.Phantoms">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer74338788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13111276135996451741">Currently rereading for the Dean Koontz group... wonder if I'll change the review? :)<br/><br/>*Didn't care for it much...and the movie didn't help much (though Peter O'Toole had some good lines). This is a straight scare fest a horror story with a good dose of splatter factor. Not my favorite of his books.*<br/><br/>Above is my first review and my 2 star rating...will I change it? No.<br/><br/>Let me say I like Koontz, he has written some books that would rate among my favorites....this isn't one. For me this is one of thos</span>
  <span id="freeText13111276135996451741" style="display:none">Currently rereading for the Dean Koontz group... wonder if I'll change the review? :)<br /><br />*Didn't care for it much...and the movie didn't help much (though Peter O'Toole had some good lines). This is a straight scare fest a horror story with a good dose of splatter factor. Not my favorite of his books.*<br /><br />Above is my first review and my 2 star rating...will I change it? No.<br /><br />Let me say I like Koontz, he has written some books that would rate among my favorites....this isn't one. For me this is one of those, "isn't this book over yet" books.<br /><br />*MINOR SPOILER BELOW*<br /><br />If I'd been in Jenny's and Lisa's place at the first of the book, by the time I'd found my second body, I'd have been headed for the sheriff's station. If I'd gotten there and found everyone dead...I'd have been in my car and headed out of town at high speed. Did these 2? NOOOO. <br /><br />Well, Lisa tried to. But her older sister, the doctor, the care giver, the one responsible for her younger (14 year old) sister keeps standing over inexplicably dead bodies saying "wait a minute" as her sister KEEPS saying "let's go!". And the book slips from there.<br /><br />I hate to say this, but I actually think I like the movie better (and it's not an exceptional movie).<br /><br />Sorry, but a forgettable novel (which may explain why I forgot it) that I was glad to see end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13111276135996451741" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_158405787" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/158405787" />
    <a title="Daniel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/365191-daniel"><img alt="Daniel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1309463474p2/365191.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/158405787?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daniel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daniel" href="/user/show/365191-daniel">Daniel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780425101452" href="/book/show/904639.Phantoms">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer158405787" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10831519541250349348">Where has this book been all of my life? And why did I write off Koontz as a hack that pushes brainless filler onto the shelves once per year? Thanks to my snobbery, I went years without picking up a book that would have satisfied my craving for a good monster story. Serves me right for thinking I knew better.<br/><br/>"Phantoms" is a marvelous, fun, and satisfying read. It has monsters; awesome, frightening, man-eating, intelligent, scary, what-in-the-world-is-going-on monsters. It is also an exciting re</span>
  <span id="freeText10831519541250349348" style="display:none">Where has this book been all of my life? And why did I write off Koontz as a hack that pushes brainless filler onto the shelves once per year? Thanks to my snobbery, I went years without picking up a book that would have satisfied my craving for a good monster story. Serves me right for thinking I knew better.<br /><br />"Phantoms" is a marvelous, fun, and satisfying read. It has monsters; awesome, frightening, man-eating, intelligent, scary, what-in-the-world-is-going-on monsters. It is also an exciting read. From the beginning, Koontz immediately launches into violence and mayhem without letting up or losing track of the greater story, which itself is a neat mash-up of historical mystery and what-if. He brings in a number of characters in a short time and with economical strokes he fleshes them out just enough to provide emotional purchase. Put shortly, this is good, solid fiction.<br /><br />I will not go into any more detail, because the story Koontz weaves together needs to be experienced without any spoilers. I will impart this advice: if you like monsters wreaking havoc in a creepy story, forget any stereotypes surrounding Koontz's work and read this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10831519541250349348" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_18394293" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/18394293" />
    <a title="William" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/997203-william"><img alt="William" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529787483p2/997203.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/18394293?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="William" class="user" itemprop="url" name="William" href="/user/show/997203-william">William</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">horror fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/997203-william?shelf=horror-fiction">horror-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer18394293&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer18394293" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13966391314589033926">This book shows both what I love and hate about Koontz. Great premises, but crappy endings.<br/><br/>For the first 70 pages or so he had me hooked. A town suddenly empty of people; Marie Celeste like food still hot on the stoves. A woman and her young sister, alone, with "something" creeping around. So far, so creepy, and I was loving it.<br/><br/>I was still with him when the cops turned up... but when the "creature" turned out to be a huge, almost omnipotent amoeba, he lost me. I stuck with it through to the end,</span>
  <span id="freeText13966391314589033926" style="display:none">This book shows both what I love and hate about Koontz. Great premises, but crappy endings.<br /><br />For the first 70 pages or so he had me hooked. A town suddenly empty of people; Marie Celeste like food still hot on the stoves. A woman and her young sister, alone, with "something" creeping around. So far, so creepy, and I was loving it.<br /><br />I was still with him when the cops turned up... but when the "creature" turned out to be a huge, almost omnipotent amoeba, he lost me. I stuck with it through to the end, but I had ceased to care about what happened to the characters by then.<br /><br />A missed opportunity. It could have been so much better.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13966391314589033926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w9bl+/1mInsJYjAfrhVGXln0LHDiTdouKjTEhy4Xwui96dumCVz8APs+Mo8s7YTQDVmFaAa+421Vj7L+GWZlfQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('y+K5szTGTIXquQ6vnAR9bVwxEGrUlQO5Fwn+Mv9Wnpi13YfuwPyS/hjlDD8e/L/jCJy5cjBmOvposohLyCc5DQ==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText1423973087529867192" style="display:none">Acknowledged as "America's most popular suspense novelist" (Rolling Stone) and as one of today's most celebrated and successful writers, Dean Ray Koontz has earned the devotion of millions of readers around the world and the praise of critics everywhere for tales of character, mystery, and adventure that strike to the core of what it means to be human.<br /><br />Dean, the author of many #1 New York Times bestsellers, lives in Southern California with his wife, Gerda, their golden retriever, Elsa, and the enduring spirit of their goldens, Trixie and Anna.<br /> <br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://Facebook.com/DeanKoontzOfficial">Facebook.com/DeanKoontzOfficial</a><br />Twitter: @DeanKoontz<br />Website: DeanKoontz.com </span>
